{1:1} kya hee dhany haai vah puroosh jo dushtton kee yuaktai par naheen chalata, aur n papiyon ke marga men khda hota aur n ttttha karanevalon kee mandlee men baaittta haai!
{1:2} parantu vah to yahova kee vyavastha se prasann rahata aur usakee vyavastha par rat din dhyan karata rahata haai.
{1:3} vah us vraksha ke saman haai, jo bahatee naliyon ke kinare lagaya gaya haai. aur apanee retu men falata haai, aur jisake patte kabhee murajhate naheen. isaliye jo kuchh vah puroosh kare vah safal hota haai..
{1:4} dushtt log aeese naheen hote, ve us boosee ke saman hote haai, jo pavan se udai jatee haai.
{1:5} is karan dushtt log adalat men sthiar n rah sakenge, aur n papee dhaarmiyon kee mandlee men ttharenge
{1:6} kyonaki yahova dharmiyon ka marga janata haai, parantu dushtton ka marga nash ho jaaega..
{2:1} jaati jati ke log kyon hullad machate haai, aur desh desh ke log vyarth baten kyon soch rahe haain?
{2:2} yahova ke aur usake aabhaishaikt ke virooddh prathvee ke raja milakar, aur haakim apas men sammaati karake kahate haai, ki
{2:3} ao, ham unake bandhan tod dale, aur unakee rassaiyon ko apane upar se utar faenke..
{2:4} vah jo svarga men virajaman haai, hansega, prabhu unako tttthon men udaaega.
{2:5} tab vah un se krodha karake baten karega, aur krodha men kahakar unhen ghabara dega, ki
{2:6} maain to apane ttharaae huae raja ko apane paavitra parvat siyyon kee rajagaee par baaitta chuka hoon.
{2:7} maain us vachan ka prachar karoonga: jo yahova ne mujh se kaha, too mera putra haai, aj too mujh se utpann hua.
{2:8} mujh se mang, aur maain jati jati ke logon ko teree sampati hone ke liye, aur door door ke deshaen ko teree nij boomi banane ke liye de doonga.
{2:9} too unhen lohe ke dnde se ttukade ttukade karega. too kumhar ke bartan kee nain unhen chakana choor kar dalega..
{2:10} isaliye ab, he rajao, buddhmaian bano he prathvee ke nyaayiyo, yah upadesh grahan karo.
{2:11} drate huae yahova kee upasana karo, aur kanpate huae magan ho.
{2:12} putra ko choomo aeesa n ho ki vah krodha kare, aur tum marga hee men nash ho jao kyonaki kshan bhr men usaka krodha bhdkane ko haai.. dhany haai ve jinaka bhrosa us par haai..
{3:1} he yahova mere satanevale kitane baddh gaae haain! vah jo mere virooddh uttte haain bahut haain.
{3:2} bahut se mere praan ke vishay men kahate haai, ki usaka bachav parameshvar kee are se naheen ho sakata.
{3:3} parantu he yahova, too to mere charon or meree ddhal haai, too meree mahima aur mere mastaishk ka uncha karanevala haai.
{3:4} maain unche shabd se yahova ko pukarata hoo, aur vah apane pavitra parvat par se mujhe uttr deta haai.
{3:5} maain lettkar so gaya fir jag utta, kyonaki yahova mujhe samhalata haai.
{3:6} maain un das hajar manushyon se naheen drata, jo mere virooddh charon or panati bandho khde haain..
{3:7} ut, he yahova! he mere parameshvar mujhe bacha le! kyonaki too ne mere sab shatrauon ke jabadon par mara haai aur too ne dushtton ke dant tod dale haain..
{3:8} uddhar yahova hee kee or se hota haai he yahova teree ashaeesh teree praja par ho..
{4:1} he mere dharmamay parameshvar, jab maain pukaroon tab too mujhe uttr de jab maain saketee men pada tab too ne mujhe vistar diya. mujh par anugrah kar aur meree praarthna sun le..
{4:2} he manushyon ke putrae, kab tak meree maahima ke badale anadar hota rahega? tum kab tak vyarth baton se praeeti rakhoge aur joottee yuktai kee khoj men rahoge?
{4:3} yah jan rakho ki yahova ne bhkt ko apane liye alag kar rakha haai jab maain yahova ko pukaroonga tab vah sun lega..
{4:4} kanpate raho aur pap mat karo apane apane bichhaune par man hee man socho aur chupachap raho.
{4:5} dharma ke balidan chaddhao, aur yahova par bhrosa rakho..
{4:6} bahut se haain jo kahate haai, ki kaun ham ko kuchh bhlai dikhaaega? he yahova too apane mukh ka prakash ham par chamaka!
{4:7} too ne mere man men us se kaheen aadhaik anand bhr diya haai, jo unako ann aur dakhmadha kee baddhtee se hotee thee.
{4:8} maain shaaantai se lett jaunga aur so jaunga kyonki, he yahova, keval too hee mujh ko aekant men nishchaint rahane deta haai..
{5:1} he yahova, mere vachanon par kan laga mere dhyan karane kee or man laga.
{5:2} he mere raja, he mere parameshvar, meree dohai par dhyan de, kyonaki maain tujhee se praarthna karata hoon.
{5:3} he yahova, bhor ko meree vanee tujhe sunai degee, maain bhor ko praarthna karake teree batt johoonga.
{5:4} kyonaki too aeesa ishvar naheen jo dushttta se prasann ho burai tere sath naheen rah sakatee.
{5:5} ghamandee tere sammukh khde hone n panaege tujhe sab anarthkariyon se gharana haai.
{5:6} too unako jo joott bolate haain nash karega yahova to hatyare aur chhlee manushy se gharana karata haai.
{5:7} parantu maain to teree apar karoona ke karan tere bhvan men aunga, maain tera bhy manakar tere pavitra maandair kee or dandvata karoonga.
{5:8} he yahova, mere shatrauon ke karan apane dharma ke marga men meree aguvai kara mere age age apane seedho marga ko dikha.
{5:9} kyonaki unake munh men koi sachchai naheen unake man men niree dushttta haai. unaka gala khulee hui kabra haai, ve apanee jeebh se chikanee chupadee baten karate haain.
{5:10} he parameshvar too unako doshaee tthara ve apanee hee yuktaiyon se ap hee gir jaaen unako unake aparadhaen kee aadhaikai ke karan nikal bahar kar, kyonaki unhon ne tujh se balava kiya haai..
{5:11} parantu jitane tujh par bhrosa rakhte haain ve sab anand kare, ve sarvada unche svar se gate rahen kyonki too unakee raksha karata haai, aur jo tere nam ke praemee haain tujh men prafauallait hon.
{5:12} kyonaki too dharmee ko aashaish dega he yahova, too usako apane anugraharoopee ddhal se ghore rahega..
{6:1} he yahova, too mujhe apane krodha men n dant, aur n jhunjhlahatt men mujhe tadna de.
{6:2} he yahova, mujh par anugrah kar, kyonki maain kumhala gaya hoon he yahova, mujhe changa kar, kyonaki meree haaddiyon men bechaainee haai.
{6:3} mera praan bhee bahut khedit haai. aur to, he yahova, kab taka?
{6:4} lautt a, he yahova, aur mere praan bacha apanee karoona ke nimitt mera uddhar kara.
{6:5} kyonaki mratyu ke bad tera smaran naheen hota adhaelok men kaun tera dhanyavad karega?
{6:6} maain karahate karahate thk gaya maain apanee khatt ansuon se bhaigota hoon prati rat mera bichhauna bheegata haai.
{6:7} meree ankhen shaek se baaittee jatee haai, aur mere sab satanevalon ke karan ve dhaundhala gai haain..
{6:8} he sab anarthkariyo mere pas se door ho kyonaki yahova ne mere rone ka shabd sun liya haai.
{6:9} yahova ne mera gidgidana suna haai yahova meree praarthna ko grahan bhee karega.
{6:10} mere sab shatra laajjait honge aur bahut ghabaraaenge ve lautt jaaenge, aur aekaaek lajjait honge..
{7:1} he mere parameshvar yahova, mera bhrosa tujh par haai sab peechha karanevalon se mujhe bacha aur chhuttkara de,
{7:2} aeesa n ho ki ve mujh ko sinh kee nai faadkar ttukade ttukade kar dalen aur koi mera chhudanevala n ho..
{7:3} he mere parameshvar yahova, yadi maain ne yah kiya ho, yaadi mere hathon se kuttlai kam hua ho,
{7:4} yaadi maain ne apane mel rakhnevalon se bhlai ke badale burai kee ho, varan maain ne usako jo akaran mera baairee tha bachaya haai
{7:5} to shatra mere praan ka peechha karake mujhe a pakade, varan mere praan ko boomi par raunde, aur meree maahima ko mittee men mila de..
{7:6} he yahova krodha karake utt mere krodhabhre satanevale ke virooddh too khda ho ja mere liye jaga! too ne nyay kee agyaa to de dee haai.
{7:7} desh desh ke logon kee mandlee tere charon or ho aur too unake upar se hokar unche sthanon par lautt ja.
{7:8} yahova samaj samaj ka nyay karata haai yahova mere dharma aur khrai ke anusar mera nyay chuka de..
{7:9} bhla ho ki dushtton kee burai ka ant ho jaa, parantu dharma ko too sthiar kara kyonki dharmee parameshvar man aur marma ka gyaata haai.
{7:10} meree ddhal parameshvar ke hath men haai, vah seedho manavalon ko bachata haai..
{7:11} parameshvar dharmee aur nyayee haai, varan aeesa ishvar haai jo praati din krodha karata haai..
{7:12} yaadi manushy n fire to vah apanee talavar par san chaddhaaega vah apana dhanush chaddhakar teer sandhaan chuka haai.
{7:13} aur us manushy ke liye us ne mratyu ke haathaiyar taaiyar kar liae haain: vah apane teeron ko aagnaiban banata haai.
{7:14} dekh dushtt ko anarth kam kee peedaaen ho rahee haai, usako utpat ka garbh haai, aur us se joott utpann hua. us ne gadha khodakar use gahira kiya,
{7:15} aur jo khai us ne banai thee us men vah ap hee gira.
{7:16} usaka utpat palatt kar usee ke sir par padega aur usaka upadrav usee ke mathe par padega..
{7:17} maain yahova ke dharma ke anusar usaka dhanyavad karoonga, aur paramapradhaan yahova ke nam ka bhjan gaunga..
{8:1} he yahova hamare prabhu, tera nam saree prathvee par kya hee pratapamay haai! too ne apana vibhv svarga par dikhaya haai.
{8:2} too ne apane baairiyon ke karan bachchon aur doodha piuvon ke dara samathrya kee nev dalee haai, taki too shatra aur palatta lenevalon ko rok rakhe.
{8:3} jab maain akash ko, jo tere hathon ka karya haai, aur chandrama aur taragan ko jo too ne niyukt kiae haai, dekhta hoon
{8:4} to fir manushy kya haai ki too usaka smaran rakhe, aur adamee kya haai ki too usakee sudhai le?
{8:5} kyonaki too ne usako parameshvar se thoda hee kam banaya haai, aur maahima aur pratap ka mukutt usake sir par rakha haai.
{8:6} too ne use apane hathon ke kayorn par prabhuta dee haai too ne usake panv tale sab kuchh kar diya haai.
{8:7} sab bhed-bakaree aur gaya-baail aur jitane vanapashu haai,
{8:8} akash ke pakshaee aur samudr kee machhliya, aur jitane jeeva-jantu samudron men chalate firate haain.
{8:9} he yahova, he hamare prabhu, tera nam saree prathvee par kya hee pratapamay haai..
{9:1} he yahova parameshvar maain apane poorn man se tera dhanyavad karoonga maain tere sab ashcharya karmon ka varnn karoonga.
{9:2} maain tere karan anaandait aur prafauallait hounga, he paramapradhaan, maain tere nam ka bhjan gaunga..
{9:3} jab mere shatra peechhe hattte haai, to ve tere samhane se ttokar khakar nash hote haain.
{9:4} kyonaki too ne mera nyay aur mukama chukaya haai too ne sinhasan par virajaman hokar dharma se nyay kiya.
{9:5} too ne anyajatiyon ko jhdika aur dushtt ko nash kiya haai too ne unaka nam anantakal ke liye mitta diya haai.
{9:6} shatra jo haai, vah mar gaa, ve anantakal ke liye ujad gaae haain aur jin nagaron ko too ne ddha diya, unaka nam va nishaan bhee mitt gaya haai.
{9:7} parantu yahova sadaaiv sinhasan par virajaman haai, us ne apana sinhasan nyay ke liye siddh kiya haai
{9:8} aur vah ap hee jagat ka nyay dharma se karega, vah desh desh ke logon ka mukama khrai se nipattaaega..
{9:9} yahova pise huon ke liye uncha gaddh ttharega, vah sankatt ke samay ke liye bhee uncha gaddh ttharega.
{9:10} aur tere nam ke jananevale tujh par bhrosa rakhenge, kyonaki he yahova too ne apane khojiyon ko tyag naheen diya..
{9:11} yahova jo siyyon men virajaman haai, usaka bhjan gao! jati jati ke logon ke beech men usake mahakamorn ka prachar karo!
{9:12} kyonaki koon ka palatta lenevala unako smaran karata haai vah deen logon kee dohai ko boolata..
{9:13} he yahova, mujh par anugrah kara. too jo mujhe mratyu ke faattkon ke pas se uttata haai, mere du: kh ko dekh jo mere baairee mujhe de rahe haain
{9:14} taaki maain siyyon ke faattkon ke pas tere sab gunon ka varnn karoo, aur tere kiae huae uddhar se magan houn..
{9:15} any jativalon ne jo gadha khoda tha, usee men ve ap gir pade jo jal unhon ne lagaya tha, us men unheen ka panv fans gaya.
{9:16} yahova ne apane ko pragatt kiya, us ne nyay kiya haai dushtt apane kiae huae kamon men fans jata haai.
{9:17} dushtt adhaelok men lautt jaaenge, tatha ve sab jatiyan bhee ja parameshvar ko bool jatee haai.
{9:18} kyonaki daridr log anantakal tak bisare huae n rahenge, aur n to namra logon kee asha sarvada ke liye nash hogee.
{9:19} ut, he parameshvar, manushy prabal n hone pae! jatiyon ka nyay tere sammukh kiya jae.
{9:20} he parameshvar, unako bhy dila! jaatiyan apane ko manushyamatra hee janen.
{10:1} he yahova too kyon door khda rahata haai? sankatt ke samay men kyon chhpai rahata haai?
{10:2} dushtton ke ahankar ke karan dee manushy khdede jate haain ve apanee hee nikalee hui yuaktaiyon men fans jaaen..
{10:3} kyonaki dushtt apanee aabhailasha par ghamand karata haai, aur lobhee parameshvar ko tyag deta haai aur usaka tiraskar karata haai..
{10:4} dushtt apane abhaiman ke karan kahata haai ki vah lekha naheen lene ka usaka poora vichar yahee haai ki koi parameshvar haai hee naheen..
{10:5} vah apane marga par draddhta se bana rahata haai tere nyay ke vichar aeese unche par hote haai, ki usakee drashtti vahan tak naheen pahunchatee jitane usake virodhaee haain un par vah faunkarata haai.
{10:6} vah apane man men kahata haai ki maain kabhee ttlane ka naheen: maain peeddhee se peeddhee tak du: kh se bacha rahoonga..
{10:7} usaka munh shaap aur chhl aur andhor se bhra haai utpat aur anarth kee baten usake munh men haain.
{10:8} vah ganvon ke ghaton men baaitta karata haai, aur gupt sthanon men nirdosh ko ghaat karata haai, usakee ankhe lachar kee ghaat men lagee rahatee haai.
{10:9} jaaisa sinh apanee jhadee men vaaisa hee vah bhee chhpaikar ghaat men baaitta karata haai vah deen ko pakadne ke liye ghaat lagaae rahata haai,
{10:10} vah deen ko apane jal men fansakar ghaseett lata haai, tab use pakad leta haai.
{10:11} vah jhuk jata haai aur vah dabak kar baaittta haai aur lachar log usake mahabalee hathon se pattke jate haain.
{10:12} vah apane man men sochata haai, ki ishvar bool gaya, vah apana munh chhpaiata haai vah kabhee naheen dekhega..
{10:13} ut, he yahova he ishvar, apana hath baddha aur deenon ko n boola.
{10:14} parameshvar ko dushtt kyon tuchchh janata haai, aur apane man men kahata haai ki too lekha n lega?
{10:15} too ne dekh liya haai, kyonki too utpat aur kalapane par duashtti rakhta haai, taaki usaka palatta apane hath men rakhe lachar apane ko tere hath men saunpata haai anathon ka too hee sahayak raha haai. dushtt kee bhuja ko tod dala
{10:16} yahova anantakal ke liye maharaj haai usake desh men se anyajati log nash ho gaae haain..
{10:17} he yahova, too ne namra logon kee aabhailasha sunee haai too unaka man taaiyar karega, too kan lagakar sunega
{10:18} ki anath aur pise huae ka nyay kare, taki manushy jo mittee se bana haai fir bhy dikhane n paae..
{11:1} mera bhrosa parameshvar par haai tum kyonaki mere praan se kahate ho ki pakshaee kee nai apane pahad par ud ja?
{11:2} kyonaki dekho, dushtt apana dhanush chaddhate haai, aur apana teer dhanush kee doree par rakhte haai, ki seedho manavalon par andhiayare men teer chalaaen.
{11:3} yaadi neven ddha dee jaaen to dharmee kya kar sakata haai?
{11:4} parameshvar apane paavitra bhvan men haai parameshvar ka sinhasan svarga men haai usakee ankhen manushy kee santan ko nit dekhtee rahatee haain aur usakee palaken unako janchatee haain.
{11:5} yahova dharmeen ko parakhta haai, parantu vah un se jo dushtt haain aur upadrav se praeeti rakhte haain apanee atma men gharana karata haai.
{11:6} vah dushtton par fande barasaaega ag aur gandhak aur prachand looh unake kattoron men bantt dee jaaengee.
{11:7} kyonaki yahova dharmee haai, vah dharma ke hee kamon se prasann rahata haai dharmeejan usaka darshan paaenge..
{12:1} he parameshvar bacha le, kyonki aek bhee bhkt naheen raha manushyon men se vishvasayogy lag mar mitte haain.
{12:2} un men se pratyek apane padosee se joottee baten kahata haai ve chapaloosee ke otton se do rangee baten karate haain..
{12:3} prabhu sab chapaloos otton ko aur us jeebh ko jis se bada bol nikalata haai katt dalega.
{12:4} ve kahate haain ki ham apanee jeebh hee se jeetenge, hamare ontt hamare hee vash men haain hamar prabhu kaun haai?
{12:5} dee logon ke lutt jane, aur daaridron ke karahane ke kara, parameshvar kahata haai, ab maain utoonga, jis par ve faunkarate haain use maain chaain vishraam doonga.
{12:6} parameshvar ka vachan pavitra haai, us chandai ke saman jo bhttee men mittee par tai gai, aur sat bar nirmal kee gai ho..
{12:7} too hee he parameshvar unakee raksha karega, unako is kal ke logon se sarvada ke liye bachaae rakhega.
{12:8} jab manushyon men neechapan ka adar hota haai, tab dushtt log charon or akadte firate haain..
{13:1} he parameshvar too kab taka? kya sadaaiv mujhe boola rahega? too kab tak apana mukhda mujh se chhpaiaae rahega?
{13:2} maain kab tak apane man hee man men yuktaiyan karata rahoo, aur din bhr apane day men duakhait raha karoo, kab tak mera shatra mujh par prabal rahega?
{13:3} he mere parameshvar yahova meree or dhyan de aur mujhe uttr de, meree ankhon men jyoti ane de, naheen to mujhe mratyu kee neend a jaaegee
{13:4} aeesa n ho ki mera shatra kahe, ki maain us par prabal ho gaya aur aeesa n ho ki jab maain dgamagane lagoon to mere shatra magan hon..
{13:5} parantu maain ne to teree karoona par bhrosa rakha haai mera day tere uddhar se magan hoga.
{13:6} maain parameshvar ke nam ka bhjan gaunga, kyonki us ne meree bhlai kee haai..
{14:1} moorkh ne apane man men kaha haai, koi parameshvar haai hee naheen. ve bigad gaa, unhon ne ghainaune kam kiae haai, koi sukarmee naheen.
{14:2} parameshvar ne svarga men se manushyon par drashtti kee haai, ki dekhe ki koi buaddhmaian, koi parameshvar ka khojee haai ya naheen.
{14:3} ve sab ke sab bhttk gaa, ve sab bhrashtt ho gaae koi sukarmee nahee, aek bhee naheen.
{14:4} kya kisee anarthkaree ko kuchh bhee gyaan naheen rahata, jo mere logon ko aeese kha jate haain jaaise rottee, aur parameshvar ka nam naheen lete?
{14:5} vahan un par bhy chha gaya, kyonaki parameshvar dharmee logon ke beech men nirantar rahata haai.
{14:6} tum to deen kee yuaktai kee hansee udate ho isaliye ki yahova usaka sharansthan haai.
{14:7} bhla ho ki israael ka uddhar siyyon se pragatt hota! jab yahova apanee praja ko dasatv se lautta le aaega, tab yakoob magan aur israael anandait hoga..
{15:1} he parameshvar tere tamboo men kaun rahega? tere paavitra parvat par kaun basane paaega?
{15:2} vah jo khrai se chalata aur dharma ke kam karata haai, aur day se sach bolata haai
{15:3} jo apanee jeebh se ninda naheen karata, aur n apane mitra kee burai karata, aur n apane padosee kee ninda sunata haai
{15:4} vah jisakee drashtti men nikamma manushy tuchchh haai, aur jo yahova ke dravaaiyon ka adar karata haai, jo shapath khakar badalata naheen chahe hani uttana pade
{15:5} jo apana roopaya byaj par naheen deta, aur nirdosh kee haani karane ke liye ghoos naheen leta haai. jo koi aeesee chal chalata haai vah kabhee n dgamagaaega..
{16:1} he ishvar meree raksha kar, kyonki maain tera hee sharanagat hoon.
{16:2} maain ne parameshvar se kaha haai, ki too hee mera prabhu haai tere sivaae meree bhlai kaheen naheen.
{16:3} prathvee par jo paavitra log haai, ve hee adar ke yogy haai, aur unheen se maain prasann hoon.
{16:4} jo paraae devata ke peechhe bhagate haain unaka du: kh baddh jaaega maain unake lohoovale tapavan naheen tapaunga aur unaka nam apane otton se naheen loonga..
{16:5} yahova mera bhag aur mere kattore ka hissa haai mere bantt ko too sthiar rakhta haai.
{16:6} mere liye map kee doree manabhavane sthan men padee, aur mera bhag manabhavana haai..
{16:7} maain yahova ko dhany kahata hoo, kyonki us ne mujhe sammaati dee haai varan mera man bhee rat men mujhe shaiksha deta haai.
{16:8} maain ne yahova ko nirantar apane sammukh rakha haai: isaliye ki vah mere daahine hath rahata haai maain kabhee n dgamagaunga..
{16:9} is karan mera day anandait aur meree atma magan hui mera shareer bhee chaain se rahega.
{16:10} kyonaki too mere praan ko adhaelok men n chhodega, n apane pavitra bhkt ko sadne dega..
{16:11} too mujhe jeevan ka rasta dikhaaega tere nikatt anand kee bhrapooree haai, tere daahine hath men sukh sarvada bana rahata haai..
{17:1} he yahova parameshvar sachchai ke vachan sun, meree pukar kee or dhyan de. meree praarthna kee or jo nishkapatt munh se nikalatee haai kan laga.
{17:2} mere mukamen ka nirny tere sammukh ho! teree ankhen nyay par lagee rahen!
{17:3} too ne mere day ko jancha haai too ne rat ko meree dekhbhal kee, too ne mujhe parakha parantu kuchh bhee khottapan naheen paya maain ne ttan liya haai ki mere munh se aparadha kee bat naheen nikalegee.
{17:4} manavee kamon men maain tere munh ke vachan ke dara krooron kee see chal se apane ko bachaae raha.
{17:5} mere panv tere pathon men sthiar rahe, fisale naheen..
{17:6} he ishvar, maain ne tujh se praarthna kee haai, kyonaki too mujhe uttr dega. apana kan meree or lagakar meree binatee sun le.
{17:7} too jo apane daahine hath ke dara apane sharangaton ko unake virodhaiyon se bachata haai, apanee adabhut karoona dikha.
{17:8} apane ankho kee putalee kee nai suraakshiat rakh apane pankhon ke tale mujhe chhpai rak,
{17:9} un dushtton se jo mujh par atyachar karate haai, mere praan ke shatrauon se jo mujhe ghore huae haain..
{17:10} unhon ne apane dayon ko kattor kiya haai unake munh se ghamand kee baten nikalatee haain.
{17:11} unhon ne pag pag par hamako ghora haai ve hamako boomi par pattk dene ke liye ghaat lagaae huae haain.
{17:12} vah us sinh kee nai haai jo apane shaikar kee lalasa karata haai, aur javan sinh kee nai ghaat lagane ke sthanon men baaitta rahata haai..
{17:13} ut, he yahova usaka samana kar aur use pattk de! apanee talavar ke bal se mere praan ko dushtt se bacha le.
{17:14} apana hath baddhakar he yahova, mujhe manushyon se bacha, arthata sansaree manushyon se jinaka bhag isee jeevan men haai, aur jinaka pett too apane bhndar se bhrata haai. ve balabachchon se santushtt haain aur shosh sampaati apane bachchon ke liye chhod jate haain..
{17:15} parantu maain to dharmee hokar tere mukh ka darshan karoonga jab maain janoonga tab tere svaroop se santushtt hoonga..
{18:1} he parameshvar, he mere bal, maain tujh se praem karata hoon.
{18:2} yahova meree chattan, aur mera gaddh aur mera chhudanevala haai mera ishvar, meree chattan haai, jisaka maain sharanagat hoo, vah meree ddhal aur meree muaktai ka gaddh haai.
{18:3} maain yahova ko jo stuati ke yogy haai pukaroonga is prakar maain apane shatrauon se bachaya jaunga..
{18:4} mratyu kee raassaiyon se maain charo or se ghair gaya hoo, aur adharma kee baddh ne mujh ko bhyabheet kar diya
{18:5} patal kee rassaiyan mere charo or thee, aur mratyu ke fande mujh par aae the.
{18:6} apane sankatt men maain ne yahova parameshvar ko pukara maain ne apane parameshvar ko dohai dee. aur us ne apane maandair men se meree baten sunee. aur meree dohai usake pas pahunchakar usake kanon men padee..
{18:7} tab prathvee hil gai, aur kanp uttee aur pahadon kee neve kanpit hokar hil gai kyonaki vah ati krodhait hua tha.
{18:8} usake nathnon se dhauan nikala, aur usake munh se ag nikalakar bhsm karane lagee jis se koele dahak utte.
{18:9} aur vah svarga ko neeche jhukakar utar aya aur usake panvon tale ghaer andhakar tha.
{18:10} aur vah karoob par savar hokar uda, varan pavan ke pankhon par savaree karake veg se uda.
{18:11} us ne aandhiayare ko apane chhpaine ka sthan aur apane charon or meghaen ke andhakar aur akash kee kalee ghattaon ka mandp banaya.
{18:12} usakee upasthiaati kee jhlak se usakee kalee ghattaen fatt gai ole aur angare.
{18:13} tab yahova akash men garaja, aur paramapradhaan ne apanee vanee sunai, ole or angare..
{18:14} us ne apane teer chala chalakar unako titar bitar kiya varan bijaaliyan gira girakar unako parast kiya.
{18:15} tab jal ke nale dekh pade, aur jagat kee neven pragatt hui, yah to yahova teree dantt se, aur tere nathnon kee sans kee jhonk se hua..
{18:16} us ne upar se hath baddhakar mujhe thanm liya, aur gaahire jal men se kheench liya.
{18:17} us ne mere balavant shatra se, aur un se jo mujh se gharana karate the mujhe chhudaya kyonaki ve adhaik samarthee the.
{18:18} meree vipaati ke din ve mujh par a pade. parantu yahova mera ashray tha.
{18:19} aur us ne mujhe nikalakar chaude sthan men pahunchaya, us ne mujh ko chhudaya, kyonaki vah mujh se prasann tha.
{18:20} yahova ne mujh se mere dharma ke anusar vyavahar kiya aur mere hathon kee shuuddhta ke anusar us ne mujhe badala diya.
{18:21} kyonaki maain yahova ke magorn par chalata raha, aur dushttta ke karan apane parameshvar se door n hua.
{18:22} kyonaki usake sare nirny meere sammukh bane rahe aur maain ne usakee vidhaiyon ko n tyaga.
{18:23} aur maain usake sammukh siddh bana raha, aur adharma se apane ko bachaae raha.
{18:24} yahova ne mujhe mere dharma ke anusar badala diya, aur mere hathon kee us shuuddhta ke anusar jise vah dekhta tha..
{18:25} dayavant ke sath too apane ko dayavant dikhata aur khre puroosh ke sath too apane ko khra dikhata haai.
{18:26} shuuddh ke sath too apane ko shuuddh dikhata, aur tteddhe ke sath too tirchha banata haai.
{18:27} kyonaki too dee logon ko to bachata haai parantu ghamand bhree ankhon ko neechee karata haai.
{18:28} ha, too hee mere deepak ko jalata haai mera parameshvar yahova mere aandhiayare ko ujiyala kar deta haai.
{18:29} kyonaki teree sahayata se maain sena par dhaava karata hoon aur apane parameshvar kee sahayata se shaharapanah ko langha jata hoon.
{18:30} ishvar ka marga sachchaai yahova ka vachan taya hua haai vah apane sab sharanagaton kee ddhal haai..
{18:31} yahova ko chhod kya koi ishvar haai? hamare parameshvar ko chhod kya aur koi chattan haai?
{18:32} yah vahee ishvar haai, jo samarth se mera kattbaindha bandhata haai, aur mere marga ko siddh karata haai.
{18:33} vahee mere paairon ko haarinaiyon ke paairon ke saman banata haai, aur mujhe mere unche sthanon par khda karata haai.
{18:34} vah mere hathon ko yuddh karana sikhata haai, isaliye meree bahon se peetal ka dhanush jhuk jata haai.
{18:35} too ne mujh ko apane bachav kee ddhal dee haai, too apane daahine hath se mujhe sambhale huae haai, aur meree namrata ne mahatv diya haai.
{18:36} too ne mere paairon ke liye sthan chauda kar diya, aur mere paair naheen fisale.
{18:37} maain apane shatrauon ka peechha karake unhen pakad loonga aur jab tab unaka ant n karoon tab tak n lautoonga.
{18:38} maain unhen aeesa bedhoonga ki ve utt n sakenge ve mere panvon ke neeche gir padenge.
{18:39} kyonaki too ne yuddh ke liye meree kamar men shaaktai ka pattuka bandha haai aur mere virodhaiyon ko mere sammukh neecha kar diya.
{18:40} too ne mere shatrauon kee peett meree or faer dee, taki maain unako katt daloon jo mujh se desh rakhte haain.
{18:41} unhon ne dohai to dee parantu unhen koi bhee bachanevala n mila, unhon ne yahova kee bhee dohai dee, parantu us ne bhee unako uttr n diya.
{18:42} tab maain ne unako koott koottkar pavan se udai hui dhooli ke saman kar diya maain ne unako galee koochon kee keechad ke saman nikal faenka..
{18:43} too ne mujhe praja ke jhgadon se bhee chhudaya too ne mujhe anyajaatiyon ka pradhaan banaya haai jin logon ko maain janata bhee n tha ve mere adhaeen ho gaye.
{18:44} mera nam sunate hee ve meree agyaa ka palan karenge paradeshaee mere vash men ho jaaenge.
{18:45} paradeshaee murjha jaaenge, aur apane kilon men se thrathrate huae nikalenge..
{18:46} yahova parameshvar jeeavit haai meree chattan dhany haai aur mere muktaidata parameshvar kee badai ho.
{18:47} dhany haai mera palatta lenevala ishvara! jis ne desh desh ke logon ko mere vansh men kar diya haai
{18:48} aur mujhe mere shatrauon se chhudaya haai too mujh ko mere virodhaiyon se uncha karata, aur upadravee puroosh se bachata haai..
{18:49} is karan maain jaati jati ke samhane tera dhanyavad karoonga, aur tere nam ka bhjan gaunga.
{18:50} vah apane ttharaae huae raja ka bada uddhar karata haai, vah apane abhaishaikt daud par aur usake vansh par yuganuyug karoona karata rahega..

{19:5} jo dulhe ke saman apane mahal se nikalata haai. vah shooraveer kee nai apanee daud daudne ko haashairt hota haai.

{19:11} aur unheen se tera das chitaya jata haai unake palan karane se bada hee praatifal milata haai.

{19:13} too apane das ko ddhttiai ke papon se bhee bachaae rakh vah mujh par prabhuta karane n paaen! tab maain siddh ho jaunga, aur bade aparadhaen se bacha rahoonga..

{20:4} vah tere man kee ichchha ko pooree kare, aur teree saree yuaktai ko sufal kare!

{22:1} he mere parameshvar, he mere parameshvar, too ne mujhe kyon chhod diya? too meree pukar se aur meree sahayat karane se kyon door rahata haai? mera uddhar kahan haai?
{22:2} he mere parameshvar, maain din ko pukarata hoon parantu too uttr naheen deta aur rat ko bhee maain chup naheen rahata.
{22:3} parantu he too jo israael kee stuti ke sihansan par virajaman haai, too to pavitra haai.
{22:4} hamare purakha tujhee par bhrosa rakhte the ve bhrosa rakhte the, aur too unhen chhudata tha.
{22:5} unhon ne teree dohai dee aur too ne unako chhudaya ve tujhee par bhrosa rakhte the aur kabhee laajjait n hue..
{22:6} parantu maain to keeda hoo, manushy naheen manushyon men meree namadharai haai, aur logon men mera apaman hota haai.
{22:7} vah sab jo mujhe dekhte haain mera ttttha karate haai, aur ontt bichakate aur yah kahate huae sir hilate haai,
{22:8} ki apane ko yahova ke vash men kar de vahee usako chhudaa, vah usako ubare kyonaki vah us se prasann haai.
{22:9} parantu too hee ne mujhe garbh se nikala jab maain doodhaapiuva bachcha tha, tab hee se too ne mujhe bhrosa rakhna sikhlaya.
{22:10} maain janmate hee tujhee par chhod diya gaya, mata ke garbh hee se too mera ishvar haai.
{22:11} mujh se door n ho kyonaki sankatt nikatt haai, aur koi sahayak naheen.
{22:12} bahut se sanddhon ne mujhe ghor liya haai, bashaan ke balavant sanddh mere charon or mujhe ghore huae haai.
{22:13} vah faadne aur garajanevale sinh kee nain mujh par apana munh pasare huae haai..
{22:14} maain jal kee nain bah gaya, aur meree sab haaddiyon ke jod ukhd gaae: mera day mom ho gaya, vah meree deh ke bheetar pighal gaya.
{22:15} mera bal toott gaya, maain tteekara ho gaya aur meree jeebh mere taloo se chipak gai aur too mujhe marakar mittee men mila deta haai.
{22:16} kyonaki kuton ne mujhe ghor liya haai kukaarmiyon kee mandlee meree charon or mujhe ghore huae haai vah mere hath aur mere paair chhedate haain.
{22:17} maain apanee sab haddiyan gin sakata hoon ve mujhe dekhte aur niharate haain
{22:18} ve mere vasr apas men banttte haai, aur mere paahirave par chitthee dalate haain.
{22:19} parantu he yahova too door n raha! he mere sahayak, meree sahayata ke liye faurtee kara!
{22:20} mere praan ko talavar se bacha, mere praan ko kutte ke panje se bacha le!
{22:21} mujhe sinh ke munh se bacha, ha, jangatee sanddhon ke seengo men se too ne mujhe bacha liya haai..
{22:22} maain apan bhaiyon ke samhane tere nam ka prachar karoonga sabha ke beech men teree prashansa karoonga.
{22:23} he yahova ke dravaaiyon usakee stuti karo! he yakoob ke vansha, tum usaka bhy mano!
{22:24} kyonaki us ne du: khee ko tuchchh naheen jana aur n us se gharana karata haai, or n us se apana mukh chhpaiata haai par jab us ne usakee dohai dee, tab usakee sun lee..
{22:25} badee sabha men mera stuti karana teree hee or se hota haai maain apane pran ko us se bhy rakhnevalon ke samhane poora karoonga
{22:26} namra log bhojan karake trapt honge jo yahova ke khojee haai, ve usakee stuati karenge. tumhare praan sarvada jeeavit rahen!
{22:27} prathvee ke sab door door deshaen ke log usako smaran karenge aur usakee or firenge aur jaati jati ke sab kul tere samhane dandvata karenge.
{22:28} kyonaki rajy yahova kee ka haai, aur sab jatiyon par vahee prabhuta karata haai..

{25:1} he yahova maain apane man ko teree or uttata hoon.

{25:4} he yahova apane marga mujh ko dikhla apana path mujhe bata de.
{25:5} mujhe apane saty par chala aur shaiksha de, kyonaki too mera udar karanevala parameshvar haai maain din bhr teree hee batt jahata rahata hoon.

{25:8} yahova bhla aur seedha haai isaaliye vah paapiyon ko apana marga dikhlaaega.
{25:9} vah namra logon ko nyay kee shaiksha deta, han vah namra logon ko apana marga dikhlaaega.

{25:11} he yahova apane nam ke nimitt mere adharma ko jo bahut haain kshama kara..
{25:12} vah kaun haai jo yahova ka bhy manata haai? yahova usako usee marga par jis se vah prasann hota haai chalaaega.
{25:13} vah kushal se ttkai rahega, aur usaka vansh prathvee par adhaikaree hoga.
{25:14} yahova ke bhed ko vahee janate haain jo us se drate haai, aur vah apanee vacha un par pragatt karega.
{25:15} meree ankhe sadaaiv yahova par ttkattkee lagaae rahatee haai, kyonki vahee mere panvon ko jal men se chhudaaega..
{25:16} he yahova meree or firakar mujh par anugrah kara kyonaki maain akela aur deen hoon.
{25:17} mere day ka klesh baddh gaya haai, too mujh ko mere du: khon se chhuda le.
{25:18} too mere du: kh aur kashtt par drashtti kar, aur mere sab papon ko kshama kara..
{25:19} mere shatrauon ko dekh ki ve kaaise baddh gaae haai, aur mujh se bada baair rakhte haain.
{25:20} mere praan kee raksha kar, aur mujhe chhuda mujhe laajjait n hone de, kyonki maain tera sharanagat hoon.
{25:21} khrai aur seedhaai mujhe surakshiat rakhe, kyonki mujhe tere hee asha haai..
{25:22} he parameshvar israael ko usake sare sankatton se chhuda le..
{26:1} he yahova, mera nyay kar, kyonki maain khrai se chalata raha hoo, aur mera bhrosa yahova par attl bana haai.
{26:2} he yahova, mujh ko janch aur parakh mere man aur day ko parakh.
{26:3} kyonaki teree karoona to meree ankhon ke samhane haai, aur maain tere saty marga par chalata raha hoon..
{26:4} maain nikammee chal chalanevalon ke sang naheen baaitta, aur n maain kapattyaien ke sath kaheen jaunga
{26:5} maain kukaarmiyon kee sangaati se gharana rakhta hoo, aur dushtton ke sang n baaitoonga..
{26:6} maain apane hathon ko nirdoshata ke jal se dhaeunga, tab he yahova maain teree vedee kee pradakshiana karoonga,
{26:7} taaki mera dhanyavad unche shabd se karoo,
{26:8} aur tere sab ashcharyakarmon ka varnn karoon.. he yahova, maain tere dhaam se teree mahima ke nivasasthan se praeeati rakhta hoon.
{26:9} mere praan ko paapiyon ke sat, aur mere jeevan ko hatyaron ke sath n mila.
{26:10} ve to ochhapan karane men lage rahate haai, aur unaka dahina hath ghoos se bhra rahata haai..
{26:11} parantu maain to khrai se chalata rahoonga. too mujhe chhuda le, aur mujh par anugrah kara.
{26:12} mere panv chauras sthan men sthiar haai sabhaon men maain yahova ko dhany kaha karoonga..
{27:1} yahova parameshvar meree jyoti aur mera uddhar haai maain kis se droon? yahova mere jeevan ka draddh gaddh tthara haai, maain kis ka bhy khaun?
{27:2} jab kukarmiyon ne jo mujhe satate aur mujhee se baair rakhte the, mujhe kha dalane ke liye mujh par chaddhai kee, tab ve hee ttokar khakar gir paden..
{27:3} chahe sena bhee mere virooddh chhavanee dale, taubhee maain n droonga chahe mere virooddh ladai ttn jaa, us dasha men bhee maain hiyav bandho nishiichat rahoonga..
{27:4} aek var maain ne yahova se manga haai, usee ke yatn men laga rahoonga ki maain jeevan bhr yahova ke bhvan men rahane pau, jis se yahova kee manoharata par drashtti lagaae rahoo, aur usake mandair men dhyan kiya karoon..
{27:5} kyonaki vah to mujhe vipaati ke din men apane mandp men chhpai rakhega apane tamboo ke guptasthan men vah mujhe chhpai lega, aur chattan par chaddhaaega.
{27:6} ab mera sir mere charon or ke shatrauon se uncha hoga aur maain yahova ke tamboo men jayajayakar ke sath baalidan chaddhaunga aur usaka bhjan gaunga..
{27:7} he yahova, mera shabd sun, maain pukarata hoo, too mujh par anugrah kar aur mujhe uttr de.
{27:8} too ne kaha haai, ki mere darshan ke khojee ho. isaliye mera man tujh se kahata haai, ki he yahova, tere darshan ka maain khojee rahoonga.
{27:9} apana mukh mujh se n chhpaia.. apane das ko krodha karake n hatta, too mera sahayak bana haai. he mere uddhar karanevale parameshvar mujhe tyag n de, aur mujhe chhod n de!
{27:10} mere mata pita ne to mujhe chhod diya haai, parantu yahova mujhe sambhal lega..
{27:11} he yahova, apane marga men meree aguvai kar, aur mere drohiyon ke karan mun ko chauras raste par le chala.
{27:12} mujh ko mere satanevalon kee ichchha par n chhod, kyonki jootte sakshaee jo upadrav karane kee dhaun men haain mere virooddh utte haain..
{27:13} yaadi mujhe vishvas n hota ki jeeviton kee prathvee par yahova kee bhlai ko dekoonga, to maain moochchhit ho jata.
{27:14} yahova kee batt johata raha hiyav bandha aur tera day draddh rahe ha, yahova hee kee batt johata raha!
{28:1} he yahova, maain tujhee ko pukaroonga he meree chattan, meree sunee anasunee n kar, aeesa n ho ki tere chup rahane se maain kabra men pade huon ke saman ho jaun jo patal men chale jate haain.
{28:2} jab maain teree dohai doo, aur tere paavitrasthan kee bheetaree kottree kee or apane hath uttau, tab meree gidgidahatt kee bat sun le.
{28:3} un dushtton aur anarthkariyon ke sang mujhe n ghaseett jo apane padosiyon se baten to mel kee bolate haain parantu day men burai rakhte haain.
{28:4} unake kamon ke aur unakee karanee kee burai ke anusar un se bartav kar, unake hathon ke kam ke anusar unhen badala de unake kamon ka palatta unhen de.
{28:5} ve yahova ke kamon par aur usake hai ke kamon par dhyan naheen karate, isaliye vah unhen pachhadega aur fir n uttaaega..
{28:6} yahova dhany haai kyonaki us ne meree gidgidahatt ko suna haai.
{28:7} yahova mera bal aur meree ddhal haai us par bhrosa rakhne se mere man ko sahayata milee haai isaaliye mera day prafaullait haai aur maain geet gakar usaka dhanyavad karoonga.
{28:8} yahova unaka bal haai, vah apane abhaishaikt ke liye uddhar ka draddh gaddh haai.
{28:9} he yahova apanee praja ka uddhar kar, aur apane nij bhag ke logon ko ashaeesh de aur unakee charavahee kar aur sadaaiv unhen sambhale raha..
{29:1} he parameshvar ke putraen yahova ka, han yahova kee ka gunanuvad karo, yahova kee maahima aur samarth ko saraho.
{29:2} yahova ke nam kee maahima karo pavitrata se shaebhayaman hokar yahova ko dandvata karo.
{29:3} yahova kee vanee meghaen ke upar sun padtee haai pratamee ishvar garajata haai, yahova ghane meghaen ke upar rahata haai.
{29:4} yahova kee vanee shaktaishaalee haai, yahova kee vanee pratapamay haai.
{29:5} yahova kee vanee devadaron ko tod dalatee haai yahova labanon ke devadaron ko bhee tod dalata haai.
{29:6} vah unhen bachhde kee nai aur labanon aur shairyon ko jangalee bachhde ke saman uchhalata haai..
{29:7} yahova kee vanee ag kee lapatton ko cheeratee haai.
{29:8} yahova kee vanee van ko hila detee haai, yahova kadesh ke van ko bhee kanpata haai..
{29:9} yahova kee vanee se harinaiyon ka garbhpat ho jata haai. aur arany men patajhd hotee haai aur usake mandair men sab koi maahima hee maahima bolata rahata haai..
{29:10} jalapralay ke samay yahova virajaman tha aur yahova sarvada ke liye raja hokar virajaman rahata haai.
{29:11} yahova apanee praja ko bal dega yahova apanee praja ko shaaantai kee ashaeesh dega..
{30:1} he yahova maain tujhe sarahoonga, kyonki too ne mujhe kheenchakar nikala haai, aur mere shatrauon ko mujh par anand karane naheen diya.
{30:2} he mere parameshvar yahova, maain ne teree dohai dee aur too ne mujhe changa kiya haai.
{30:3} he yahova, too ne mera praan adhaelok men se nikala haai, too ne mujh ko jeeavit rakha aur kabra men padne se bachaya haai..
{30:4} he yahova ke bhkto, usaka bhjan gao, aur jis pavitra nam se usaka smaran hota haai, usaka dhanyavad karo.
{30:5} kyonaki usaka krodha, to kshan bhr ka hota haai, parantu usakee prasannata jeevan bhr kee hotee haai. kadaachita rat ko rona pade, parantu sabere anand pahunchega..
{30:6} maain ne to chaain ke samay kaha tha, ki maain kabhee naheen ttlane ka.
{30:7} he yahova apanee prasannata se too ne mere pahad ko draddh aur sthiar kiya tha jab too ne apana mukh faer liya tab maain ghabara gaya..
{30:8} he yahova maain ne tujhee ko pukara aur yahova se gidgidakar yah binatee kee, ki
{30:9} jab maain kabra men chala jaunga tab mere lohoo se kya labh hoga? kya mittee tera dhanyavad kar sakatee haai? kya vah teree sachchai ka prachar kar sakatee haai?
{30:10} he yahova, sun, mujh par anugrah kara he yahova, too mera sahayak ho..
{30:11} too ne mere liye vilap ko nraty men badal dala, too ne mera ttatt utaravakar meree kamar men anand ka pattuka bandha haai
{30:12} taaki meree atma tera bhjan gatee rahe aur kabhee chup n ho. he mere parameshvar yahova, maain sarvada tera dhanyavad karata rahoonga..
{31:1} he yahova mera bhrosa tujh par haai mujhe kabhee laajjait hona n pade too apane dharmee hone ke karan mujhai chhuda le!
{31:2} apana kan meree or lagakar turant mujhe chhuda le!
{31:3} kyonaki too ne mere liye chattan aur mera gaddh haai isaliye apane nam ke nimitt meree aguvai kar, aur mujhe age le chala.
{31:4} jo jal unhon ne mere liye bichhaya haai us se too mujh ko chhuda le, kyonki too hee mera draddh gaddh haai.
{31:5} maain apanee atma ko tere hee hath men saunp deta hoon he yahova, he satyavadee ishvar, too ne mujhe mol lekar mukt kiya haai..
{31:6} jo vyarth vastuon par man lagate haai, un se maain gharana karata hoon parantu mera bhrosa yahova hee par haai.
{31:7} maain teree karoona se magan aur anaandait hoo, kyonki too ne mere du: kh par drashtti kee haai, mere kashtt ke samay too ne meree suadhai lee haai,
{31:8} aur too ne mujhe shatra ke hath men padne naheen diya too ne mere panvon ko chaude sthan men khda kiya haai..
{31:9} he yahova, mujh par anugrah kar kyonaki maain sankatt men hoon meree ankhe varan mera praan aur shareer sab shaek ke mare ghaule jate haain.
{31:10} mera jeevan shaek ke mare aur meree avastha karahate karahate ghatt chalee haai mera bal mere adharma ke karan jata rah, or meree haaddiyan ghaul gai..
{31:11} apane sab virodhaiyon ke karan mere padosiyon men meree namadharai hui haai, apane janapahichanavalon ke liye dr ka karan hoon jo mujh ko sadk par dekhte haai vah mujh se door bhag jate haain.
{31:12} maain mratak kee nai logon ke man se bisar gaya maain tootte basan ke saman ho gaya hoon.
{31:13} maain ne bahuton ke munh se apana apavad suna, charon or bhy hee bhy haai! jab unhon ne mere virooddh apas men sammati kee tab mere praan lene kee yuaktai kee..
{31:14} parantu he yahova maain ne to tujhee par bhrosa rakha haai, maain ne kaha, too mera parameshvar haai.
{31:15} mere din tere hath men haai too mujhe mere shatrauon aur mere satanevalon ke hath se chhuda.
{31:16} apane das par apane munh ka prakash chamaka apanee karoona se mera uddhar kara..
{31:17} he yahova, mujhe lajjait n hone de kyonki maain ne tujh ko pukara haai dushtt laajjait hon aur ve patal men chupachap pade rahen.
{31:18} jo anhakar aur apaman se dharmee kee ninda karate haai, unake joott bolanevale munh band kiae jaaen..
{31:19} aha, teree bhlai kya hee badee haai jo too ne apane dravaaiyon ke liye rakh chhodee haai, aur apane sharanagaton ke liye manushyon ke samhane pragatt bhee kee haai!
{31:20} too unhen darshan dene ke guptasthan men manushyon kee buree goshttee se gupt rakhega too unako apane mandp men jhgade-ragade se chhpai rakhega..
{31:21} yahova dhany haai, kyonaki us ne mujhe gaddhvale nagar men rakhkar mujh par addhbhut karoona kee haai.
{31:22} maain ne to ghabarakar kaha tha ki maain yahova kee draashtti se door ho gaya. taubhee jab maain ne teree dohai dee, tab too ne meree gidgidahatt ko sun liya..
{31:23} he yahova ke sab bhkton us se praem rakho! yahova sachche logon kee to raksha karata haai, parantu jo ahankar karata haai, usako vah bhlee bhanati badala deta haai.
{31:24} he yahova par asha rakhnevalon hiyav bandhaen aur tumhare day draddh rahen!
{32:1} kya hee dhany haai vah jisaka aparadha kshama kiya gaya, aur jisaka pap ddhapa gaya ho.
{32:2} kya hee dhany haai vah manushy jisake adharma ka yahova lekha n le, aur jisakee atma men kapatt n ho..
{32:3} jab maain chup raha tak din bhr kaharate kaharate meree haaddiyan pighal gai.
{32:4} kyonaki rat din maain tere hath ke neeche daba raha aur meree taravatt dhoop kal kee see jhurrahatt banatee gai..
{32:5} jab maain ne apana pap tujh par pragatt kiya aur apana adharma n chhpaiaya, aur kaha, maain yahova ke samhane apane aparadhaen ko man loonga tab too ne mere adharma aur pap ko kshama kar diya..
{32:6} is karan har aek bhkt tujh se aeese samay men praarthna kare jab ki too mil sakata haai. nishchay jab jal kee badee baddh aae taubhee us bhkt ke pas n pahunchegee.
{32:7} too mere chhpaine ka sthan haai too sankatt se meree raksha karega too mujhe charon or se chhuttkare ke geeton se ghor lega..
{32:8} maain tujhe buaddh idoonga, aur jis marga men tujhe chalana hoga us men teree aguvai karoonga maain tujh par krapadraashtti rakoonga aur sammati diya karoonga.
{32:9} tum ghaede aur khchchar ke saman n bano jo samajh naheen rakhte, unakee umang lagam aur bag se rokanee padtee haai, naheen to ve tere vash men naheen apane ke..
{32:10} dushtt ko to bahut peeda hogee parantu jo yahova par bhrosa rakhta haai vah karoona se ghaira rahega.
{32:11} he dhaarmiyon yahova ke karan anaandait aur magan ho, aur he sab seedho manavalon anand se jayajayakar karo!
{33:1} he dhaarmiyon yahova ke karan jayajayakar karo kyonnki dharmee logon ko stuati karanee sohatee haai.
{33:2} veena baja bajakar yahova ka dhanyavad karo, das taravalee sarangee baja bajakar usaka bhjan gao.
{33:3} usake liye naya geet gao, jayajayakar ke sath bhlee bhanati bajao..
{33:4} kyonaki yahova ka vachan seedha haai aur usaka sab kam sachchai se hota haai.
{33:5} vah dharma aur nyay se praeeti rakhta haai yahova kee karoona se prathvee bhrapoor haai..
{33:6} akashamandl yahova ke vachan se, aur usake sare gan usake munh hee shvas se bane.
{33:7} vah samudr ka jal ddher kee nai ikattha karata vah gaahire sagar ko apane bhndar men rakhta haai..
{33:8} saree prathvee ke log yahova se dre, jagat ke sab nivasee usaka bhy manen!
{33:9} kyonaki jab us ne kaha, tab ho gaya jab us ne agyaa dee, tab vastav men vaaisa hee ho gaya..
{33:10} yahova anyajayien kee yuaktai ko vyarth kar deta haai vah desh desh ke logon kee kalpanaon ko nishfal karata haai.
{33:11} yahova kee yuaktai sarvada sthiar rahegee, usake man kee kalpanaaen peeddhee se peeddhee tak banee rahengee.
{33:12} kya hee dhany haai vah jaati jisaka parameshvar yahova haai, aur vah samaj jise us ne apana nij bhag hone ke liye chun liya ho!
{33:13} yahova svarga se draashtti karata haai, vah sab manushyon ko niharata haai
{33:14} apane nivas ke sthan se vah prathvee ke sab rahanevalon ko dekhta haai,
{33:15} vahee jo un sabhon ke dayon ko gaddhta, aur unake sab kamon ka vichar karata haai.
{33:16} koi aeesa raja nahee, jo sena kee bahutayat ke karan bach sake veer apanee badee shaktai ke karan choott naheen jata.
{33:17} bach nikalane ke liye ghaeda vyarth haai, vah apane bade bal ke dara kisee ko naheen bacha sakata haai..
{33:18} dekho, yahova kee drashtti usake dravaaiyon par aur un par jo usakee karoona kee asha rakhte haain banee rahatee haai,
{33:19} ki vah unake praan ko mratyu se bachaa, aur akal ke samay unako jeevit rakhe..
{33:20} ham yahova ka asara dekhte aae haain vah hamara sahayak aur hamaree ddhal tthara haai.
{33:21} hamara day usake karan anaandait hoga, kyonaki ham ne usake pavitra nam ka bhrosa rakha haai.
{33:22} he yahova jaaisee tujh par hamaree asha haai, vaaisee hee teree karoona bhee ham par ho..
{34:1} maain har samay yahova ko dhany kaha karoonga usakee stuati nirantar mere mukh se hotee rahegee.
{34:2} maain yahova par ghamand karoonga namra log yah sunakar anaandait honge.
{34:3} mere sath yahova kee badai karo, aur ao ham milakar usake nam kee stuati karen.
{34:4} maain yahova ke pas gaya, tab us ne meree sun lee, aur mujhe pooree reeati se nirbhy kiya.
{34:5} jinhon ne usakee or drashtti kee unhon ne jyoti pai aur unaka munh kabhee kala n hone paya.
{34:6} is deen jan ne pukara tab yahova ne sun liya, aur usako usake sab kashtton se chhuda liya..
{34:7} yahova ke dravaaiyon ke charon or usaka doot chhavanee kiae huae unako bachata haai.
{34:8} parakhkar dekho ki yahova kaaisa bhla haai! kya hee dhany haai vah puroosh jo usakee sharan leta haai.
{34:9} rahe yahova ke pavitra logo, usaka bhy mano, kyonaki usake dravaaiyon ko kisee bat kee ghattee naheen hotee!
{34:10} javan sihon ko to ghattee hotee aur ve bookhe bhee rah jate haain parantu yahova ke khojiyon ko kisee bhlee vastu kee ghattee n hovegee..
{34:11} he ladko, ao, meree suno, maain tum ko yahova ka bhy manana sikhaunga.
{34:12} vah kaun manushy haai jo jeevan kee ichchha rakhta, aur deegharayu chahata haai taaki bhlai dekhe?
{34:13} apanee jeebh ko burai se rok rak, aur apane munh kee chaukasee kar ki us se chhl kee bat n nikale.
{34:14} burai ko chhod aur bhlai kara mel ko ddoonddh aur usee ka peechha kara..
{34:15} yahova kee ankhe dhaarmiyon par lagee rahatee haai, aur usake kan bhee usakee dohai kee or lage rahate haain.
{34:16} yahova burai karanevalon ke vimukh rahata haai, taki unaka smaran prathvee par se mitta dale.
{34:17} dharmee dohai dete haain aur yahova sunata haai, aur unako sab vipaatiayon se chhudata haai.
{34:18} yahova tootte manavalon ke sameep rahata haai, aur pise huon ka udar karata haai..
{34:19} dharmee par bahut see vipaatiayan padtee to haai, parant yahova usako un sab se mukt karata haai.
{34:20} vah usakee haddee haddee kee raksha karata haai aur un men se aek bhee toottne naheen patee.
{34:21} dushtt apanee burai ke dara mara jaaega aur dharmee ke baairee doshaee ttharenge.
{34:22} yahova apane dason ka praan mol lekar bacha leta haai aur jitane usake sharanagat haain un men se koi bhee doshaee n ttharega..
{35:1} he yahova jo mere sath mukama ladte haai, unake sath too bhee mukama lad jo mujh se yud karate haai, un se too yud kara.
{35:2} ddhal aur bhala lekar meree sahayata karane ko khda ho.
{35:3} barchhee ko kheench aur mera peechha karanevalon ke samhane akar unako roka aur mujh se kah, ki maain tera udar hoon..
{35:4} jo mere praan ke graahak haain ve lajjait aur niradar hon! jo meree hati kee kalpana karate haai, vah peechhe hattaae jaaen aur unaka munh kala ho!
{35:5} ve vayu se ud janevalee boosee ke saman ho, aur yahova ka doot unhen hankata jaae!
{35:6} unaka marga andhiayara aur fisalaha ho, aur yahova ka doot unako khdedta jae..
{35:7} kyonaki akaran unhon ne mere liye apana jal gadhe men bichhaya akaran hee unhon ne mera praan lene ke liye gadha khoda haai.
{35:8} achanak un par vipaati a pade! aur jo jal unhon ne bichhaya haai usee men ve ap hee fanse aur usee vipaati men ve ap hee paden!
{35:9} parantu maain yahova ke karan apane man men magan hounga, maain usake kiae huae udar se hashairt hounga.
{35:10} meree haddee haddee kahengee, he yahova tere tuly kaun haai, jo dee ko bade bade balavanton se bachata haai, aur lutteron se deen daaridr logon kee raksha karata haai?
{35:11} jootte sakshaee khde hote haain aur jo bat maain naheen janata, vahee mujh se poochhte haain.
{35:12} ve mujh se bhlai ke badale burai karate haain yahan tak ki mera praan ub jata haai.
{35:13} jab ve rogee the tab to maain ttatt paahine raha, aur upavas kar karake du: kh uttata raha aur meree praarthna ka fal meree god men lautt aya.
{35:14} maain aeesa bhav rakhta tha ki mano ve mere sangee va bhai haain jaaisa koi mata ke liye vilap karata ho, vaaisa hee maain ne shaek ka paahirava pahine huae sir jhukakar shaek kiya..
{35:15} parantu jab maain langadane laga tab ve log anandait hokar ikatthe hua, neech log aur jinhen maain janata bhee n tha ve mere virood ikatthe huae ve mujhe lagatar faadte rahe
{35:16} un pakhndee bhandon kee nai jo pett ke liye upahas karate haai, ve bhee mujh par dant peesate haain..

{57:1} he parameshvar, mujh par anugrah kar, mujh par anugrah kar, kyonki maain tera sharanagat hoon aur jab tak ye apatiayan nikal n jaae, tab tak maain tere pankhon ke tale sharan liae rahoonga.

{67:1} parameshvar ham par anugrah kare aur ham ko ashaeesh de vah ham par apane mukh ko prakash chamakaae

{68:1} parameshvar utte, usake shatra tittr bitar hon aur usake baairee usake samhane se bhag jaaen.
{68:2} jaaise dhauan ud jata haai, vaaise hee too unako uda de jaaise mom ag kee anch se pighal jata haai, vaaise hee dushtt log parameshvar kee upaasthiaati se nash hon.
{68:3} parantu dharmee anandait hon ve parameshvar ke samhane prafauallait hon ve anand se magan hon!
{68:4} parameshvar ka geet gao, usake nam ka bhjan gao jo nirjal deshaen men savar hokar chalata haai, usake liye sadk banao usaka nam yah haai, isaliye tum usake samhane prafauallait ho!
{68:5} parameshvar apane paavitra dhaam me, anathon ka pita aur vidhavaon ka nyayee haai.
{68:6} parameshvar anathon ka ghar basata haai aur bandhauon ko chhudakar bhagyavan karata haai parantu hatteelon ko sookhee boomi par rahana padta haai..

{68:8} tab prathvee kanp uttee, aur akash bhee parameshvar ke samhane ttpakane laga, udhar seenaai parvat parameshvar, han israael ke parameshvar ke samhane kanp utta.
{68:9} he parameshvar, too ne bahut se varadan barasaae tera nij bhag to bahut sookha tha, parantoo too ne usako hara bhra kiya haai
{68:10} tera jhund us men basane laga he parameshvar too ne apanee bhlai se deen jan ke liye taaiyaree kee haai.
{68:11} prabhu agyaa deta haai, tab shuubh samachar sunanevaaliyon kee badee sena ho jatee haai.
{68:12} apanee apanee sena samet raja bhage chale jate haai, aur grahaasthian loott ko bantt letee haai.
{68:13} kya tum bhedshaalon ke beech lett jaoge? aur aeesee kabootaree ke saman hoge jisake pankh chandee se aur jisake par peele sone se maddhe huae hon?
{68:14} jab sarvashaaktaiman ne us men rajaon ko tittr bitar kiya, tab mano salmon parvat par him pada..
{68:15} bashaan ka pahad parameshvar ka pahad haai bashaan ka pahad bahut shaikhravala pahad haai.
{68:16} parantu he shaikhravale pahado, tum kyon us parvat ko ghoorate ho, jise parameshvar ne apane vas ke liye chaha haai, aur jahan yahova sada vas kiae rahega?
{68:17} parameshvar ke rath bees hajar, varan hajaron hajar haain prabhu unake beech men haai, jaaise vah seenaai pavitrasthan men haai.
{68:18} too unche par chaddha, too logon ko bandhauvai men le gaya too ne manushyon se, varan hatteele manushyon se bhee bhentten lee, jis se yah parameshvar un men vas kare..
{68:19} dhany haai prabhu, jo praati din hamara bojh uttata haai vahee hamara uddharakarta ishvar haai.
{68:20} vahee hamare liye bachanevala ishvar tthara yahova prabhu mratyu se bhee bachata haai..
{68:21} nishchay parameshvar apane shatrauon ke sir par, aur jo adharma ke rmag par chalata rahata haai, usake bal bhre chonden par mar mar ke use choor karega.
{68:22} prabhu ne kaha haai, ki maain unhen bashaan se nikal launga, maain unako gaahire sagar ke tal se bhee faer le aunga,
{68:23} ki too apane panv ko lohoo men duboa, aur tere shatra tere kuton ka bhag ttharen..
{68:24} he paramashevar teree gati dekhee gai, mere ishvar, mere raja kee gati pavitrasthan men dikhai dee haai
{68:25} ganevale age age aur taravale bajon ke bajanevale peechhe peechhe gaa, charon or kumaariyan dfa bajatee theen.
{68:26} sabhaon men parameshvar ka, he israael ke sote se nikale huae logo, prabhu ka dhanyavad karo.
{68:27} vahan unako adhyaksha chhotta binyameen haai, vahan yahooda ke hakim apane anucharon samet haai, vahan jabooloon aur naptalee ke bhee hakim haain..
{68:28} tere parameshvar ne agyaa dee, ki tujhe samathrya mile he parameshvar jo kuchh too ne hamare liye kiya haai, use draddh kara.
{68:29} tere mandair ke karan jo yarooshalem men haai, raja tere liye bhentt le aaenge.
{68:30} narakatton men rahanevale banaaile pashuuon ko, sandon ke jhund ko aur desh desh ke bachhdon ko jhdik de. ve chandee ke ttukade liye huae pranam karenge jo loge yuddh se prasann rahate haai, unako us ne titar bitar kiya haai.
{68:31} misr se rais aaenge kooshaee apane hathon ko parameshvar kee or faurtee se faailaaenge..

{68:33} jo sab se unche sanatan svarga men savar hokar chalata haai dekho vah apanee vanee sunata haai, vah gambheer vanee shaktaishaalee haai.

{68:35} he parameshvar, too apane pavitrasthanon men bhyayogy haai, israael ka ishvar hee apanee praja ko samathrya aur shaaktai ka denevala haai. parameshvar dhany haai..
{69:1} he parameshvar, mera uddhar kar, maain jal men ooba jata hoon.
{69:2} maain bade daladal men dhasa jata hoo, aur mere paair kaheen naheen rookate maain gaahire jal men a gaya, aur dhaara men ooba jata hoon.
{69:3} maain pukarate pukarate thk gaya, mera gala sookh gaya haai apane parameshvar kee batt johate johate, meree ankhe rah gai haain..
{69:4} jee akaran mere baairee haai, ve ginatee men mere sir ke balon se aadhaik haain mere vinash karanevale jo vyarth mere shatra haai, ve samartheen haai, isaaliye jo maain ne lootta naheen vah bhee mujh ko dena pada haai.

{69:13} parantu he yahova, meree praarthna to teree prasannata ke samay men ho rahee haai he parameshvar apanee karoona kee bahutayat se, aur bachane kee apanee sachchee praatigyaa ke anusar meree sun le.
{69:14} mujh ko daladal men se ubar, ki maain dhans n jaun maain apane baaiariyon se, aur gaahire jal men se bach jaun.
{69:15} maain dhaara men oob n jau, aur n maain gahire jal men oob maroo, aur n patal ka munh mere upar band ho..
{69:16} he yahova, meree sun le, kyonki teree karoona uttm haai apanee daya kee bahutayat ke anusar meree or dhyan de.
{69:17} apane das se apana munh n mod kyonki maain sankatt men hoo, faurtee se meree sun le.
{69:18} mere nikatt akar mujhe chhuda le, mere shatrauon se mujh ko chhuttkara de..
{69:19} meree namadharai aur lajja aur anadar ko too janata haai: mere sab draehee tere samhane haain.
{69:20} mera day namadharai ke karan fatt gaya, aur maain bahut udas hoon. maain ne kisee taras khanevale kee asha to kee, parantu kisee ko n paya, aur shaantai denevale ddoonddhta to raha, parantu koi n mila.
{69:21} aur logon ne mere khane ke liye indraayan diya, aur meree pyas bujhane ke liye mujhe siraka pilaya..
{69:22} unako bhojan unake liye fanda ho jae aur unake sukh ke samay jal ban jae.
{69:23} unakee ankhon par andhora chha jaa, taki ve dekh n saken aur too unakee kaatt iko nirantar kanpata raha.
{69:24} unake upar apana rosh bhdka, aur tere krodha kee anch unako lage.
{69:25} unakee chhavanee ujad jaa, unake deron men koi n rahe.

{70:1} he parameshvar mujhe chhudane ke liye, he yahova meree sahayata karane ke liye faurtee kara!
{70:2} jo mere praan ke khojee haai, unakee asha tootte, aur munh kala ho jaae! jo meree hani se prasann hote haai, ve peechhe hattaae aur niradar kiae jaaen.
{70:3} jo kahate haai, aha, aha, ve apanee lajja ke mare ulatte faere jaaen..

{71:1} he yahova maain tera sharanagat hoon meree asha kabhee toottne n paae!

{71:11} parameshvar ne usako chhod diya haai usaka peechha karake use pakad lo, kyonki usaka koi chhudanevala naheen..

{71:19} aur he parameshvar, tera dharma ati mahan haai.. too jis ne mahakarya kiae haai, he paramevar tere tuly kaun haai?
{71:20} too ne to ham ko bahut se kattnai kashtt dikhaae haain parantu ab too fir se ham ko jilaaega aur prathvee ke gahire gadhe men se ubar lega.

{72:1} he parameshvar, raja ko apana niyam bata, rajaputra ko apana dharma sikhla!

{72:3} pahadon aur pahadiyon se praja ke liye, dharma ke dara shaantai mila karegee
{72:4} vah praja ke deen logon ka nyay karega, aur daridra logon ko bachaaega aur andhor karanevalon ko choor karega..
{72:5} jab tak soorya aur chandrama bane rahenge tab tak log peeddhee-peeddhee tera bhy manate rahenge.
{72:6} vah ghaas kee koonttee par barasanevale menh, aur boomi seenchanevalee jhaadiyon ke saman hoga.

{74:1} he parameshvar, too ne hamen kyon sada ke liye chhod diya haai? teree kopagnai ka dhauan teree charai kee bhendon ke virooddh kyon utt raha haai?
{74:2} apanee mandlee ko jise too ne praacheenakal men mol liya tha, aur apane nij bhag ka gotra hone ke liye chhuda liya tha, aur is siyyon parvat ko bhee, jis par too ne vas kiya tha, smaran kara!
{74:3} apane dg sanatan kee khndhar kee or baddha arthata un sab buraiyon kee or jo shatrara ne pavitrasthan men kiae haain..
{74:4} tere draehee tere sabhasthan ke beech garajate rahe haain unhon ne apanee hee dhvajaon ko chinh ttharaya haai. ve un manushyon ke saman the
{74:5} jo ghane van ke pedon par kulhade chalate haain.
{74:6} aur ab ve us bhvan kee nakkashaee ko, kulhaadyaien aur hathaudon se bilakul tode dalate haain.
{74:7} unhon ne tere pavitrasthan ko ag men jhonk diya haai, aur tere nam ke nivas ko girakar ashuuddh kar dala haai.
{74:8} unhon ne man men kaha haai ki ham inako ekadak daba den unhon ne is desh men ishvar ke sab sabhasthanon kon foonk diya haai..
{74:9} ham ko hamare nishaan naheen dekh padte ab koi nabee naheen raha, n hamare beech koi janata haai ki kab tak yah dasha rahegee.
{74:10} he parameshvar draehee kab tak namadharai karata rahega? kya shatra, tere nam kee ninda sada karata rahega?
{74:11} too apana daahina hath kyon roke rahata haai? use apane panjar se nikal kar unaka ant kar de..
{74:12} parameshvar to praacheenakal se mera raja haai, vah prathvee par uddhar ke kam karata aya haai.
{74:13} too ne apanee shaaktai se samudra ko do bhag kar diya too ne jal men magaramachchhon ke siron ko faod diya.
{74:14} too ne to livyatanon ke sir ttukade ttukade karake jangalee jantuon ko khaiala diae.
{74:15} too ne to sota kholakar jal kee dhaara bahai, too ne to barahamasee nadiyon ko sukha dala.
{74:16} din tera haai rat bhee teree haai soorya aur chandrama ko too ne sthiar kiya haai.
{74:17} too ne to prathvee ke sab sivanon ko ttharaya dhoopakal aur jada donon too ne ttharaae haain..
{74:18} he yahova smaran kar, ki shatra ne namadharai hee haai, aur mooddh logon ne tere nam kee ninda kee haai.

{92:7} ki dushtt jo ghaas kee nain foolate-falate haai, aur sab anarthkaree jo prafauallait hote haai, yah isaaliye hota haai, ki ve sarvada ke liye nash ho jaae,

{104:12} unake pas akash ke pakshaee basera karate, aur daliyon ke beech men se bolate haain.
{104:13} too apanee attariyon men se pahadon ko seenchata haai tere kamon ke fal se prathvee trapt rahatee haai..

{104:15} aur dakhmadha jis se manushy ka man anaandait hota haai, aur tel jis se usaka mukh chamakata haai, aur ann jis se vah sambhl jata haai.

{104:17} un men chidiyan apane ghaensale banatee haain lagalag ka basera sanauvar ke vrakshaen men hota haai.
{104:18} unche pahad jangalee bakaron ke liye haain aur chattanen shaapanon ke sharansthan haain.

{104:20} too andhakar karata haai, tab rat ho jatee haai jis men van ke sab jeev jantu ghoomate firate haain.
{104:21} javan sinh aher ke liye garajate haai, aur ishvar se apana ahar mangate haain.
{104:22} soorya uday hote hee ve chale jate haain aur apanee mandon men ja baaittte haain.
{104:23} tab manushy apane kam ke liye aur sandhya tak parishram karane ke liye nikalata haai.

{119:74} tere dravaaiye mujhe dekhkar anandait honge, kyonki maain ne tere vachan par asha lagai haai.

{119:76} mujhe apanee karoona se shaaantai de, kyonki too ne apane das ko aeesa hee vachan diya haai.
{119:77} teree daya mujh par ho, tab maain jeevit rahoonga kyonki maain teree vyavastha se sukhee hoon.
{119:78} aabhaimaaniyon kee asha tootte, kyonki unhon ne mujhe joott ke dara gira diya haai parantu maain tere upadeshaen par dhyan karoonga.
{119:79} jo tera bhy manate haai, vah meree or fire, tab ve teree chitauaniyon ko samajh lenge.
{119:80} mera man teree vidhaiyon ke manane men siddh ho, aeesa n ho ki mujhe laajjait hona pade..
{119:81} mera praan tere uddhar ke liye baaichen haai parantu mujhe tere vachan par asha rahatee haai.
{119:82} meree ankhen tere vachan ke poore hone kee batt johate johate rah gain haai aur maain kahata hoon ki too mujhe kab shaantai dega?
{119:83} kyonaki maain dhooaen men kee kuppee ke saman ho gaya hoo, taubhee teree vidhaiyon ko naheen boola.
{119:84} tere das ke kitane din rah gaae haain? too mere peechhe pade huon ko dand kab dega?
{119:85} aabhaimanee jo taree vyavastha ke anusar naheen chalate, unhon ne mere liye gadhe khode haain.
{119:86} teree sab agyaaaen vishvasayogy haain ve log joott bolate huae mere peechhe pade haain too meree sahayata kara!
{119:87} ve mujh ko prathvee par se mitta dalane hee par the, parantu maain ne tere upadeshaen ko naheen chhoda.
{119:88} apanee karoona ke anusar mujh ko jila, tab maain teree dee hui chitaunee ko manoonga..
{119:89} he yahova, tera vachan, akash men sada tak sthiar rahata haai.
{119:90} teree sachchai peeddhee se peeddhee tak banee rahatee haai too ne prathvee ko sthiar kiya, isaliye vah banee haai.
{119:91} ve aj ke din tak tere niyamon ke anusar tthare haain kyonki saree sraashtti tere adhaeen haai.
{119:92} yaadi maain teree vyavastha se sukhee n hota, to maain du: kh ke samay nash ho jata.
{119:93} maain tere upadeshaen ko kabhee n booloonga kyonki unheen ke dara too ne mujhe jilaya haai.
{119:94} maain tera hee hoo, too mera uddhar kara kyonaki maain tere upadeshaen kee sudhai rakhta hoon.
{119:95} dushtt mera nash karane ke liye meree ghaat men lage haain parantu maain teree chitauaniyon par dhyan karata hoon.
{119:96} jitanee baten pooree jan padtee haai, un sab ko to maain ne adhooree paya haai, parantu teree agyaa ka vistar bada haai..
{119:97} aha! maain teree vyavastha men kaaisee praeeati rakhta hoon! din bhr mera dhyan usee par laga rahata haai.
{119:98} too apanee agyaaon ke dara mujhe apane shatrauon se adhaik buddhmaian karata haai, kyonki ve sada mere man men rahatee haain.
{119:99} maain apane sab shaikshakon se bhee adhaik samajh rakhta hoo, kyonki mera dhyan teree chitauaniyon par laga haai.
{119:100} maain puraaniyon se bhee samajhdar hoo, kyonki maain tere upadeshaen ko pakade huae hoon.
{119:101} maain ne apane panvon ko har aek bure raste se rok rakha haai, jis se maain tere vachan ke anusar chaloon.
{119:102} maain tere niyamon se naheen hatta, kyonki too hee ne mujhe shaiksha dee haai.
{119:103} tere vachan mujh ko kaaise meette lagate haai, ve mere munh men madha se bhee meette haain!
{119:104} tere upadeshaen ke karan maain samajhdar ho jata hoo, isaaliye maain sab mithya margon se baair rakhta hoon..
{119:105} tera vachan mere panv ke liye deepak, aur mere marga ke liye ujiyala haai.
{119:106} maain ne shapath khai, aur ttana bhee haai ki maain tere dharmapay niyamon ke anusar chaloonga.

{119:108} he yahova, mere vachanon ko svechchhabali janakar grahan kar, aur apane niyamon ko mujhe sikha.
{119:109} mera praan nirantar meree hathelee par rahata haai, taubhee maain teree vyavastha ko bool naheen gaya.

{119:114} too meree ad aur ddhal haai meree asha tere vachan par haai.
{119:115} he kukarmiyo, mujh se door ho jao, ki maain apane parameshvar kee agyaaon ko pakade rahoon.

{119:126} vah samay aya haai, ki yahova kam kare, kyonaki logon ne teree vyavastha ko tod diya haai.

{132:9} tere yajak dharma ke vasr paahine rahe, aur tere bhkt log jayajayakar karen.
{132:10} apane das daud ke liye apane aabhaishaikt kee praarthna kee anasunee n kara..
{132:11} yahova ne daud se sachchee shapath khai haai aur vah us se n mukarega: ki maain teree gaee par tere aek nij putra ko baaittaunga.

{132:13} kyonaki yahova ne siyyon ko apanaya haai, aur use apane nivas ke liye chaha haai..

{133:1} dekho, yah kya hee bhlee aur manohar bat haai ki bhai log apas men mile rahen!

{135:1} yah kee stuti karo, yahova ke nam kee stuti karo, he yahova ke sevako tum stuti karo,

{136:1} yahova ka dhanyavad karo, kyonaki vah bhla haai, aur usakee karoona sada kee haai.

{137:1} babul kee naharon ke kinare ham log baaitt gaa, aur siyyon ko smaran karake ro pade!

{145:12} ki ve adaamiyon par tere parakram ke kam aur tere rajy ke pratap kee maahima pragatt karen.
{145:13} tera rajy yug yug ka aur teree prabhuta sab peeddhiyon tak banee rahegee..

{145:15} sabhon kee ankhen teree or lagee rahatee haai, aur too unako ahar samay par deta haai.
{145:16} too apanee mutthee kholakar, sab praanaiyon ko ahar se trapt karata haai.
{145:17} yahova apanee sab gaati men dharmee aur apane sab kamon me karoonamay haai.
{145:18} jinate yahova ko pukarate haai, arthata jitane usako sachchai se pukarate hen un sabhon ke vah nikatt rahata haai.
{145:19} vah apane dravaaiyon kee ichchha pooree karata haai, or unakee dohai sunakar unaka uddhar karata haai.
{145:20} yahova apane sab praemiyon kee to raksha karata, parantu sab dushtton ko satyanash karata haai..

{146:1} yah kee stuti karo. he mere man yahova kee stuati kara!
{146:2} maain jeevan bhr yahova kee stuti karata rahoonga jab tak maain bana rahoonga, tab tak maain apane parameshvar ka bhjan gata rahoonga..
{146:3} tum pradhaanon par bhrosa n rakhna, n kisee adamee par, kyonki us men uddhar karane kee bhee shaaktai naheen.
{146:4} usaka bhee praan nikalega, vahee bhee mittee men mil jaega usee din usakee sab kalpanaen nash ho jaengee..
{146:5} kya hee dhany vah haai, jisaka sahayak yakoob ka ishvar haai, aur jisaka bhrosa apane parameshvar yahova par haai.
{146:6} vah akash aur prathvee aur samudra aur un men jo kuchh haai, sab ka karta haai aur vah apana vachan sada ke liye poora karata rahega.

{146:8} yahova andhaen ko ankhen deta haai. yahova jhuke huon ko seedha khda karata haai yahova dharmiyon se praem rakhta haai.

{146:10} he siyyon, yahova sada ke liye, tera parameshvar peeddhee peeddhee rajy karata rahega. yah kee stuti karo!
{147:1} yah kee stuti karo! kyonaki apane parameshvar ka bhjan gana achchha haai kyonaki vah manabhavana haai, usakee stuti karanee manabhavanee haai.
{147:2} yahova yarooshalem ko basa raha haai vah nikale huae israaeliyon ko ikattha kar raha haai.
{147:3} vah kheadit manavalon ko changa karata haai, aur unake shaek par marahama-pattee bandhata haai.
{147:4} vah taron ko ginata, aur un men se aek aek ka nam rakhta haai.
{147:5} hamara prabhu mahan aur aati samarthee haai usakee buaddh iaparampar haai.
{147:6} yahova namra logon ko sambhlata haai, aur dushtton ko boomi par gira deta haai..
{147:7} dhanyavad karate huae yahova ka geet gao veena bajate huae hamare parameshvar ka bhjan gao.
{147:8} vah akash ko meghaen se chha deta haai, aur prathvee ke liye menh kee taaiyaree karata haai, aur pahadon par ghaas ugata haai.
{147:9} vah pashuuon ko aur kauve ke bachchon ko jo pukarate haai, ahar deta haai.
{147:10} n to vah ghaede ke bal ko chahata haai, aur n puroosh ke paairon se prasann hota haai
{147:11} yahova apane dravaaiyon hee se prasann hota haai, arthata un se jo usakee karoona kee asha lagaae rahate haain..
{147:12} he yarooshalem, yahova kee prashansa kara! he siyyon, apane parameshvar kee stuti kara!
{147:13} kyonaki us ne tere faattkon ke khmbhon ko draddh kiya haai aur tere ladke balon ko ashaeesh dee haai.
{147:14} aur tere sivanon men shaaantai deta haai, aur tujh ko uttm se uttm gehoon se trapt karata haai.
{147:15} vah prathvee par apanee agyaa ka prachar karata haai, usaka vachan aati veg se daudta haai.
{147:16} vah un ke saman him ko girata haai, aur rakh kee nain pala bikherata haai.
{147:17} vah barfa ke ttukade girata haai, usakee kee hui ttnd ko kaun sah sakata haai?
{147:18} vah agyaa dekar unhen galata haai vah vayu bahata haai, tab jal bahane lagata haai.
{147:19} vah yakoob ko apana vachan, aur israael ko apanee vidhaiyan aur niyam batata haai.
{147:20} kisee aur jaati se us ne aeesa bartav naheen kiya aur usake niyamon ko auron ne naheen jata.. yah kee stuati karo.
{148:1} yah kee stuti karo! yahova kee stuti svarga men se karo, usakee stuti unche sthanon men karo!
{148:2} he usake sab dooto, usakee stuati karo: he usakee sab sena usakee stuati kara!
{148:3} he soorya aur chandrama usakee stuati karo, he sab jyotimay taragan usakee stuti karo!
{148:4} he sab se unche akasha, aur he akash ke uparavale jal, tum donon usakee stuti karo.
{148:5} ve yahova ke nam kee stuti kare, kyonki usee ne agyaa dee aur ye siraje gaae.
{148:6} aur us ne unako sada sarvada ke liye sthiar kiya haai aur aeesee vidhai ttharai haai, jo ttlane kee naheen..
{148:7} prathvee men se yahova kee stuti karo, he magaramachchhon aur gahire sagar,
{148:8} he aagnai aur olo, he him aur kuhare, he usaka vachan mananevalee prachand bayara!
{148:9} he pahadon aur sab tteelo, he faladai vrakshaen aur sab devadaron!
{148:10} he vana-pashuuon aur sab gharaailoo pashuuo, he renganevale jantuon aur he pakshiayon!
{148:11} he prathvee ke rajao, aur rajy rajy ke sab logo, he hakimon aur prathvee ke sab nyayiyon!
{148:12} he javanon aur kumariyo, he puraaniyon aur balakon!
{148:13} yahova ke nam kee stuti karo, kyonaki keval usakee ka nam mahan haai usaka aeeshvarya prathvee aur akash ke upar haai.
{148:14} aur us ne apanee praja ke liye aek seeng uncha kiya haai yah usake sab bhkton ke liye arthata israaeliyon ke liye aur usake sameep rahanevalee praja ke liye stuti karane ka vishay haai. yah kee stuati karo.
{149:1} yah kee stuti karo! yahova ke liye naya geet gao, bhkton kee sabha men usakee stuati gao!
{149:2} israael apane kartta ke karan anaandait ko, siyyon ke nivasee apane raja ke karan magan hon!
{149:3} ve nachate huae usake nam kee stuati kare, aur dfa aur veena bajate huae usaka bhjan gaaen!
{149:4} kyonaki yahova apanee praja se prasann rahata haai vah namra logon ka uddhar karake unhen shaebhayaman karega.
{149:5} bhkt log mahima ke karan prafauallait hon aur apane bichhaunon par bhee pade pade jayajayakar karen.
{149:6} unake kantt se ishvar kee prashansa ho, aur unake hathon men dodhaaree talavaren rahe,
{149:7} ki ve anyajaatiyon se palatta le saken aur rajy rajy ke logon ko tadna de,
{149:8} aur unake rajaon ko sankalon se, aur unake pratishttit purooshaen ko lohe kee bediyon se jakad rakhe,
{149:9} aur unako ttharaya hua dand den! usake sab bhkton kee aeesee hee pratishtta hogee. yah kee stuti karo.

{150:2} usake parakram ke kamon ke karan usakee stuti karo usakee atyant badai ke anusar usakee stuti karo!
{150:3} narasinga foonkate huae usakee stuti karo sarangee aur veena bajate huae usakee stuati karo!
{150:4} dfa bajate aur nachate huae usakee stuati karo taravale baje aur bansulee bajate huae usakee stuti karo!
